页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

arXiv:2509.26285v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：交变磁体具有两个关键特征：非相对论性交替自旋分裂（即交变磁力）和依赖于材料的 Néel 向量。前者与 Rashba 自旋轨道耦合 (SOC) 自然地共存于基底上的真实材料中，引发了 SOC 如何影响交流磁体的磁性的问题。后者对于信息存储至关重要，因此确定其方向至关重要。为了解决这些问题，我们通过独立改变 Néel 矢量方向和 SOC 强度来研究二维 (2D) d 波交流磁体中的 Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida (RKKY) 相互作用。我们的结果表明，Néel 向量方向可以在没有 SOC 的情况下通过 Ising 项准确确定，或者通过有 SOC 的 DM 项定性推断。此外，我们观察到一种与之前报道不同的新型 Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya (DM) 成分，其出现归因于交变磁性和 SOC 之间的协同作用。此外，通过调整 SOC 强度，我们揭示了由五种不同机制控制的 RKKY 自旋模型的演变：自旋模型可能仅由交变磁性、仅由 SOC 或仅由动力学项确定；或者，交变磁力可能会同时产生与 SOC 相同的中等各向异性自旋模型，或者与 SOC 竞争产生具有最大各向异性的自旋模型。除了 SOC 强度之外，哪种机制的运行还依赖于 Néel 矢量方向和杂质配置。所有结果均经过数值验证。这些发现——由于一阶 SOC 展开和固定 Néel 向量方向的限制，在之前的研究中是无法获得的——为交流磁体的磁性提供了重要的新见解。

English Abstract

arXiv:2509.26285v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Altermagnets possess two key features: non-relativistic alternating spin splitting (i.e., altermagnetism) and a material-dependent Néel vector. The former naturally coexists with Rashba spin-orbit coupling (SOC) in real materials on substrates, prompting the question of how SOC affects the magnetic properties of altermagnets. The latter is crucial for information storage, making it essential to determine its orientation. To address these issues, we study the Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida (RKKY) interaction in two-dimensional (2D) d-wave altermagnets by independently varying the Néel vector orientation and the SOC strength. Our results demonstrate that the Néel vector orientation can be accurately determined via the Ising term without SOC, or qualitatively inferred via the DM terms with SOC. Moreover, we observe a novel Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya (DM) component distinct from previous reports, whose emergence is attributed to the synergy between altermagnetism and SOC. Additionally, through tuning SOC strength, we reveal the evolution of the RKKY spin models governed by five distinct mechanisms: the spin model may be determined solely by altermagnetism, solely by SOC, or solely by the kinetic term; alternatively, altermagnetism may coincidentally yield the same moderately anisotropic spin model as SOC, or compete with SOC to produce a spin model with maximal anisotropy. Beyond SOC strength, which mechanism operates also relies on the Néel vector orientation and impurity configurations. All results are numerically verified. These findings -- which were inaccessible in prior studies due to the limitations of first-order SOC expansion and fixed Néel vector orientation -- provide important new insights into the magnetic properties of altermagnets.

长冈铁磁体在方形和三角形晶格交叉中的自旋螺旋不稳定性#

Spin-spiral instability of the Nagaoka ferromagnet in the crossover between square and triangular lattices

中文摘要

arXiv:2510.05226v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：我们研究半填充附近方形和三角形晶格交叉中的核心 Fermi-Hubbard 模型。正如 Nagaoka 在 20 世纪 60 年代所认识到的那样，在方形晶格上，单孔的存在会导致铁磁自旋有序。在三角晶格上，几何挫败反而导致自旋单重基态，这可以与 120 度螺旋级相关。在正方形和三角形之间插值的晶格上，存在相变，在该相变中铁磁序变得不稳定而成为自旋螺旋。我们对这种转变进行建模，找到自旋螺旋不稳定性的确切位置。

English Abstract

arXiv:2510.05226v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: We study the hard-core Fermi-Hubbard model in the crossover between square and triangular lattices near half-filling. As was recognized by Nagaoka in the 1960s, on the square lattice the presence of a single hole leads to ferromagnetic spin ordering. On the triangular lattice, geometric frustration instead leads to a spin-singlet ground state, which can be associated with a 120-degree spiral order. On lattices which interpolate between square and triangular, there is a phase transition at which the ferromagnetic order becomes unstable to a spin spiral. We model this transition, finding the exact location of the spin-spiral instability.

arXiv:2512.18611v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：有限磁场中方形晶格的铁磁 Ising 模型的配分函数是使用启发式图论方法中的拓扑考虑因素推导出来的。这些方程针对低温和高温状态分别推导，而当磁场为零时，从中获得 Onsager 的精确解。这里导出的配分函数方程几乎与 Onsager 给出的方程相似，因此表明即使存在磁场，协议也很简单。这里使用亥姆霍兹自由能导出的自发磁化强度与精确解产生的自发磁化强度相同。配分函数导致已知的磁化强度和零场磁化率的级数展开。

English Abstract

arXiv:2512.18611v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: The partition functions of ferromagnetic Ising models of square lattices in a finite magnetic field is deduced using topological considerations within a heuristic graph-theoretical approach. These equations are derived separately for low and high temperature regimes while the exact solution of Onsager is obtained therefrom when the magnetic field is zero. The derived partition function equations here are almost similar to those given by Onsager, thus indicating a straight-forward protocol, even when the magnetic field is present. The spontaneous magnetization derived here using the Helmholtz free energy is identical with that arising from the exact solution. The partition functions lead to the known series expansions of the magnetization and zero-field susceptibility.

磁学的另一章#

An alternate chapter in magnetism
📚 Nature Physics📅 2026-01-15⚡ 磁性/铁电

阅读原文 ↗
页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

最近提出的一类磁体，即所谓的交替磁体，结合了铁磁体和反铁磁体的特征。我们讨论交流磁体的科学吸引力、当前的争议和实际应用的挑战。磁性材料有多种形式。铁磁和反铁磁化合物在基础研究和实际应用中都受到了最多的关注。铁磁体的自旋沿相同方向排列，产生强磁场，而反铁磁体具有相反的自旋，相互抵消，导致没有净磁化。最近，研究人员发现了一种新的磁相，称为交变磁相。交变磁体于 20221 年首次提出，它汇集了铁磁和反铁磁秩序的定义方面。与铁磁体一样，它们表现出电子带的自旋相关分裂（如图）——这意味着自旋向上和自旋向下的电子占据稍微不同的能级——同时保持零净磁化强度，这是反铁磁性的标志。这些特征是由对称驱动的自旋排列和通过镜像或旋转对称连接的相反自旋子晶格引起的。这种配置也打破了时间反转对称性。根据理论建议，对 MnTe 的角分辨光电子能谱研究揭示了相当大的能带分裂，这是交变磁性的关键特征2,3。然而，仅能带分裂可能不足以将材料归类为交流磁体。在《自然物理学》最近的一篇评论中，刘启航及其同事认为，为了牢固地建立交变磁序，连接具有相反磁矩的亚晶格的对称操作必须既不是反转也不是平移4。这强调了在对新的交磁化合物进行分类时将光谱证据与严格的对称性分析相结合的重要性。并非所有最初提出作为交流磁体的材料都经受住了详细的审查。例如，最近对 RuO2 的研究——曾经被认为是一种有前途的候选者 5——没有发现磁序的证据 6。然而，探索该化合物磁性基态的研究表明，内部应变可能在确定特定 RuO2 样品是否磁性有序方面发挥关键作用7。这些发现引发了关于交变磁体表征的持续争论，强调了样品纯度以及明确的交变磁体行为实验和理论标准的重要性。在铁磁体中，描述磁有序程度的有序参数等于净磁化强度。然而，在交流磁体中，由于潜在的对称性限制，情况更加复杂。这引发了研究界的积极讨论，试图解决交流磁体的阶次参数是什么。最近的研究提出，磁多极可以作为交变磁行为的定义有序参数8。这个想法促使实验学家开发测量这些多极点的方法，并促使理论学家建立对潜在机制的全面理解。从应用的角度来看，铁磁体和反铁磁体各有其优点和局限性。铁磁体可产生自旋极化电流，其净磁化强度使其对于数据存储和磁传感器非常有价值。然而，它们也会通过杂散磁场产生噪声，并且它们的商业化面临可扩展性问题。相比之下，反铁磁体具有针对小磁场扰动的鲁棒性和超快自旋动力学，可实现更快的运行，但它们缺乏自旋极化电流，限制了它们在自旋电子学中的使用，自旋电子学使用基于自旋的机制而不是单独的电荷。交替磁铁有可能通过结合两者的特点来克服这些问题。交流磁体的自旋分裂能带结构产生反常电子传输响应，例如反常霍尔效应和磁光克尔效应，而不需要自旋轨道耦合。这对于自旋电子器件应用很有帮助。交变磁体的快速自旋动力学和对称驱动的传输使其成为存储设备、逻辑门和传感器的理想选择。研究人员正在探索它们在太赫兹纳米振荡器和自旋扭矩设备中的应用，太赫兹纳米振荡器对于超快无线通信非常有用，而自旋扭矩设备对于节能存储器和逻辑电路非常重要。此外，它们独特的能带结构也可能导致拓扑相和奇异的准粒子9。除了潜在的技术应用之外，它们的对称性还可能为基础凝聚态研究开辟新的研究方向。在持续的争论和实验挑战中，交流磁体的前景仍在评估中。目前的大部分工作仍然是理论上的或仅限于一些实验系统。主要挑战包括合成合适的材料、了解它们在环境条件下的行为并将它们集成到设备架构中。未来应用的另一个关键要求是在室温下表现出交变磁性能的金属化合物的可用性。最近的一项研究成功证明了此类材料的存在10。尽管交流磁体在科学上很有趣，但它们是否真的会开启磁性的新篇章将取决于实验和理论的进展，以及它们在实际应用中相对于现有磁性材料的优势的明确证明。 Šmejkal, L.、Sinova, J. 和 Jungwirth, T.Phys。修订版 X12, 031042 (2022)。谷歌学术 Krempaský, J. et al.Nature626, 517–522 (2024)。文章ADSGoogle Scholar Osumi, T. et al.Phys.修订版 B109, 115102 (2024)。文章ADSGoogle 学者 Liu, Q.、Dai, X. 和 Blügel, S.Nat。物理学.21, 329–331 (2025)。文章谷歌学者 Feng, Z. 等人，Nat。电子.5，735–743（2022）。文章Google Scholar Keßler, P. et al.npj Spintronics2, 50 (2024)。文章谷歌学者 Jeong, S. English Abstract

A recently proposed class of magnets, so-called altermagnets, combine features of ferromagnets and antiferromagnets. We discuss the scientific appeal of altermagnets, current controversies and challenges for their practical use. Magnetic materials come in many forms. Ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic compounds have received the most attention for both fundamental research and practical applications. The spins of ferromagnets align in the same direction, creating a strong magnetic field, whereas antiferromagnets have opposite spins that cancel each other out, resulting in no net magnetization. Recently, researchers have discovered a new magnetic phase called altermagnetism. First proposed in 20221, altermagnets bring together defining aspects of ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic order. Like ferromagnets, they exhibit spin-dependent splitting of electronic bands (pictured) — meaning spin-up and spin-down electrons occupy slightly different energy levels — while maintaining zero net magnetization, a hallmark of antiferromagnetism. These features are caused by a symmetry-driven spin arrangement with opposite-spin sublattices that are connected by mirror or rotational symmetry1. This configuration also breaks time-reversal symmetry. Following the theoretical proposal, angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy studies on MnTe revealed considerable band splitting, a key signature of altermagnetism2,3. However, band splitting alone may not be sufficient to classify a material as an altermagnet. In a recent Comment inNature Physics, Qihang Liu and colleagues argued that to firmly establish altermagnetic order, the symmetry operations connecting sublattices with opposite magnetic moments must be neither inversion nor translation4. This underscores the importance of combining spectroscopic evidence with rigorous symmetry analysis when classifying new altermagnetic compounds. Not all materials initially proposed as altermagnets have withstood detailed scrutiny. For example, recent investigations of RuO2— once considered a promising candidate5— found no evidence of magnetic order6. However, studies exploring the magnetic ground state in this compound revealed that internal strain may play a critical role in determining whether the particular RuO2sample orders magnetically or not7. These findings have sparked an ongoing debate on the characterization of altermagnets, highlighting the importance of sample purity and well-defined experimental and theoretical criteria for altermagnetic behaviour. In ferromagnets, the order parameter, which describes the degree of magnetic order, equals the net magnetization. However, in altermagnets, the situation is more complex because of the underlying symmetry restrictions. This has led to active discussions within the research community trying to resolve what the order parameter of an altermagnet is. Recent studies have proposed that magnetic multipoles may serve as the defining order parameter for altermagnetic behaviour8. This idea has motivated experimentalists to develop methods for measuring these multipoles7and theorists to build a comprehensive understanding of the underlying mechanisms. From the standpoint of applications, ferromagnets and antiferromagnets each have their strengths and limitations. Ferromagnets enable spin-polarized currents and their net magnetization makes them valuable for data storage and magnetic sensors. However, they also produce noise through stray magnetic fields and their commercialization faces scalability issues. In contrast, antiferromagnets offer robustness against small magnetic field perturbations and ultrafast spin dynamics for faster operation, but they lack spin-polarized currents, limiting their use in spintronics, which uses spin-based mechanisms instead of charge alone. Altermagnets have the potential to overcome these issues by combining features of both. The spin-split band structure of altermagnets produces anomalous electronic transport responses, such as the anomalous Hall effect and magneto-optical Kerr effect, without needing spin–orbit coupling. This is helpful for spintronic device applications. Their fast spin dynamics and symmetry-driven transport make altermagnets ideal for memory devices, logic gates and sensors. Researchers are exploring their use in terahertz nano-oscillators, which are useful for ultrafast wireless communication, and spin-torque devices, which are important for energy-efficient memory and logic circuits. Furthermore, their unique band structures may also lead to topological phases and exotic quasiparticles9. Apart from potential technological applications, their symmetry properties may open new research directions in fundamental condensed-matter research. The prospects for altermagnets are still being assessed amid ongoing debate and experimental challenges. Much of the current work remains theoretical or limited to a few experimental systems. Key challenges include synthesizing suitable materials, understanding their behaviour under ambient conditions and integrating them into device architectures. Another key requirement for future applications is the availability of metallic compounds exhibiting altermagnetic properties at room temperature. A recent study has successfully demonstrated the existence of such materials10. Although altermagnets are scientifically intriguing, whether they will indeed open a new chapter in magnetism will depend on experimental and theoretical progress and a clear demonstration of their advantages over existing magnetic materials in practical applications. 在室温下操纵一个滑动铁电晶体管内的数千个非易失性极化状态#

Manipulating thousands of non-volatile polarization states within one sliding ferroelectric transistor at room temperature

阅读原文 ↗
页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

在单个铁电器件中创建多个偏振态可用于神经形态计算，以提高计算分辨率。然而，在室温下，此类系统中稳定偏振态的数量通常限于 32 个。在这里，我们报告了在室温下在滑动铁电晶体管中操纵数千个非易失性偏振态，该晶体管由六方氮化硼顶部的对齐石墨烯单层组成。仅由源极-漏极脉冲调节，可以在一种掺杂水平下产生超过 36 个准连续偏振态。在源极-漏极脉冲期间叠加栅极电压可以在84个掺杂水平之间可逆地调节石墨烯费米能量，将物理上不同的极化态数量提升到3,024个（36个状态×84个掺杂水平）。这些偏振态可以维持超过 105 秒，并且有可能持续 10 年。丰富的偏振态可能源于极性域壁的运动和局部注入载流子的莫尔势。使用 3,024 个偏振态在深度残差网络中进行训练期间量化的模拟显示了时尚图像的浮点可比识别精度（约 93.53%）。

English Abstract

Creating multiple polarization states in a single ferroelectric device is of use in neuromorphic computing to enhance computational resolution. However, the number of stable polarization states in such systems is typically limited to 32 at room temperature. Here we report the manipulation of thousands of non-volatile polarization states at room temperature in a sliding ferroelectric transistor that is composed of an aligned graphene monolayer atop hexagonal boron nitride. Solely regulated by source–drain pulses, more than 36 quasi-continuous polarization states can be generated at one doping level. Superimposing a gate voltage during the source–drain pulses can reversibly regulate the graphene Fermi energy between 84 doping levels, promoting the number of physically distinct polarization states to 3,024 (36 states × 84 doping levels). These polarization states can sustain for over 105s and could potentially persist for 10 years. The abundant polarization states probably stem from the motion of polar domain walls and the moiré potential localizing the injected carriers. The simulation of during-training quantization in a deep residual network using the 3,024 polarization states shows a floating-point-comparable recognition accuracy (around 93.53%) for fashion images.

[原始信息] Nature Electronics, Published online: 14 January 2026; doi:10.1038/s41928-025-01551-7 Using 36 polarization states generated at 84 doping levels, 3,024 physically distinct polarization states can be achieved at room temperature in a sliding ferroelectric transistor that is composed of an aligned graphene monolayer atop hexagonal boron nitride.

三角形反铁磁体中的几何自旋#

Geometric Spin Rotation in Triangular Antiferromagnets

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.07914v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们描述了一种几何现象，其中由简并戈德斯通模式组成的行波留下了变换后的基态。在三角形海森堡反铁磁体中，圆偏振自旋波脉冲使自旋在其平面内旋转。非线性运动方程的精确解表明，累积旋转是与阶次参数的平行传输相关的几何相位。我们指出了磁序参数的运动与摆动硬币的运动之间的一个奇怪的类比。这种现象开辟了一条通过自旋波控制反铁磁序的新途径，并且可能扩展到其他受挫磁体以及具有非交换对称破缺发生器的其他物理系统。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.07914v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We describe a geometric phenomenon in which a traveling wave made of degenerate Goldstone modes leaves behind a transformed ground state. In a triangular Heisenberg antiferromagnet, a pulse of circularly polarized spin waves rotates the spins within their plane. An exact solution of the nonlinear equations of motion demonstrates that the accumulated rotation is a geometric phase related to parallel transport of the order parameter. We point out a curious analogy between the motion of the magnetic order parameter and that of a wobbling coin. This phenomenon opens a new route for controlling antiferromagnetic order by spin waves and may extend to other frustrated magnets as well as other physical systems with noncommuting broken-symmetry generators.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.08117v1 发布类型：新 摘要：自旋方向或纹理的节能快速切换是自旋电子学的核心问题，需求量很大，但仍然具有挑战性。与基于自旋转移力矩或自旋轨道力矩的主流路线不同，我们提出了另一种称为磁电力矩的机制，通过纯电场来切换极性磁双层中的磁化强度。在一些磁性范德华双层中，当极化的静电能可以补偿层间磁耦合时，会产生磁电扭矩，在几皮秒内快速翻转自旋，这一点通过结合第一性原理计算、解析模型以及原子模拟得到了证明。这种磁电扭矩不依赖于自旋轨道耦合，并且通常在极性磁同质结构和异质结构中活跃。我们的工作提供了一种在纳米尺度上切换磁化强度的替代途径，这可能有利于节能和快速响应的自旋电子器件。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08117v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Energy-efficient fast switching of spin orientations or textures is a core issue of spintronics, which is highly demanded but remains challenging. Different from the mainstream routes based on spin-transfer torque or spin-orbit torque, here we propose another mechanism coined as magnetoelectric torque to switch the magnetization in polar magnetic bilayers via pure electric field. In some magnetic van der Waals bilayers, when the electrostatic energy of polarization can compensate the interlayer magnetic coupling, a magnetoelectric torque is generated to fastly flip spins within a few picoseconds, which is demonstrated by combining the first-principles calculations, analytic model, as well as atomistic simulations. Such a magnetoelectric torque doesn't rely on the spin-orbit coupling and is generally active in polar magnetic homostructures and heterostructures. Our work provides an alternative route to switch magnetization in nanoscale, which may benefit the energy-saving and fast-response spintronic devices.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.08232v1 公告类型：新 摘要：非晶合金软磁性能的微观起源从根本上与局部拓扑无序和磁交换相互作用之间的相互作用有关。在这项工作中，我们采用多尺度自旋晶格动力学 (SLD) 方法来研究非晶 CoₓFe₁₋ₓ 纳米盘 (x=35, 50, 65) 中的磁结构相关性。通过将经典分子动力学与广义磁哈密顿量相结合，我们捕获了晶格振动和自旋进动之间的动态反馈回路。通过 Voronoi 镶嵌进行的拓扑分析揭示了持久的物种依赖性结构异质性：钴原子优先采用“类固体”二十面体堆积，形成刚性结构主链，而铁原子则表现出更高的“类液体”无序环境倾向。我们证明这种拓扑差异决定了宏观磁响应。钴驱动的结构刚度保留了强大的交换网络，可最大限度地提高饱和磁化强度，而富铁区域固有的局部无序会引入交换波动，充当内在的阻尼机制，从而延迟磁弛豫。这些发现为Co-Fe金属玻璃中铁磁有序的稳定性提供了原子学解释，并为通过化学计量控制调节非晶自旋电子器件中的阻尼参数提供了途径。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08232v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The microscopic origin of soft magnetic properties in amorphous alloys is fundamentally linked to the interplay between local topological disorder and magnetic exchange interactions. In this work, we employ a multiscale Spin-Lattice Dynamics (SLD) approach to investigate the magnetostructural correlations in amorphous CoₓFe₁₋ₓ nanodisks (x=35, 50, 65). By integrating classical molecular dynamics with a generalized magnetic Hamiltonian, we capture the dynamic feedback loop between lattice vibrations and spin precession. Topological analysis via Voronoi tessellation reveals a persistent species-dependent structural heterogeneity: Cobalt atoms preferentially adopt "solid-like" icosahedral packing, forming a rigid structural backbone, whereas Iron atoms exhibit a higher propensity for "liquid-like" disordered environments. We demonstrate that this topological disparity dictates the macroscopic magnetic response. The Cobalt-driven structural stiffness preserves a robust exchange network that maximizes saturation magnetization, while the local disorder inherent to Iron-rich regions introduces exchange fluctuations that act as an intrinsic damping mechanism, delaying magnetic relaxation. These findings provide an atomistic explanation for the stability of ferromagnetic order in Co-Fe metallic glasses and offer a pathway for tuning damping parameters in amorphous spintronic devices through stoichiometric control.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.08239v1 公告类型：新 摘要：由于拓扑和磁性之间的强烈相互作用，Kagome 磁体表现出一系列新颖且重要的拓扑特性，这也延伸到了它们的热电应用。磁性拓扑材料研究的最新进展凸显了它们有趣的反常霍尔效应和热电效应，这些效应主要源于大的固有贝里曲率。在这里，我们报告了在 kagome 反铁磁体 (AFM) ErMn6Sn6 中观察到 Sₓy^A ~ 1.3 μV K⁽⁻¹⁾ 的大室温 (RT) 反常能斯特效应 (ANE)，这与已知磁性材料中观察到的最大信号相当。令人惊讶的是，我们进一步发现，RT 处显着的拓扑能斯特信号，在 180 K 处峰值约为 0.2 μV K⁽⁻¹⁾，与螺旋 AFM 状态下的 ANE 完全耦合，源于由不相称的自旋结构引起的实空间非零自旋手性。这项研究展示了基于能斯特效应的潜在室温热电应用平台，并为发现不相称的 AFM 系统中显着的异常和拓扑横向输运效应提供了见解。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08239v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Kagome magnets exhibit a range of novel and nontrivial topological properties due to the strong interplay between topology and magnetism, which also extends to their thermoelectric applications. Recent advances in the study of magnetic topological materials have highlighted their intriguing anomalous Hall and thermoelectric effects, arising primarily from large intrinsic Berry curvature. Here, we report observation of a large room-temperature (RT) anomalous Nernst effects (ANE) of Sₓy^A ~ 1.3 μV K⁽⁻¹⁾ in the kagome antiferromagnet (AFM) ErMn6Sn6, which is comparable to the largest signals observed in known magnetic materials. Surprisingly, we further found that a significant topological Nernst signal at RT and peaking a maximum of approximately 0.2 μV K⁽⁻¹⁾ at 180 K, exactly coupling with ANE in the spiral AFM state, originates from the real-space nonzero spin chirality caused by incommensurate spin structure. This study demonstrates a potential room-temperature thermoelectric application platform based on Nernst effect, and provides insights for discovering significant anomalous and topological transverse transport effects in the incommensurate AFM system.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.08317v1 公告类型：新 摘要：人们已经根据布洛赫能带和杂质散射的几何性质来理解反常霍尔效应，并且在铁磁体和反铁磁体等各种磁性材料中观察到了反常霍尔效应。最近，在非共线反铁磁金属NbMnP中报道了大的反常霍尔效应，其磁序是偶宇称和奇宇称磁性成分的混合。这种磁结构预计会因反铁磁体有序性的对称性破缺而表现出反常霍尔效应和非线性霍尔效应。在这里，我们利用第一性原理计算和 Wannier 插值方法从理论上研究了 Bloch 带的量子几何结构引起的 NbMnP 固有的反常和非线性霍尔效应。我们发现 NbMnP 的本征霍尔响应主要受特定镜面上强烈增强的贝里曲率和贝里连接偏振偶极子的控制。这些增强的几何量源自自旋轨道耦合引起的沿节点线的间隙开口。我们的结果表明，NbMnP 可作为研究源于宇称混合反铁磁体中的节点线的输运现象的模型系统。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08317v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The anomalous Hall effect has been understood in terms of the geometric nature of Bloch bands and impurity scattering, and has been observed in a wide variety of magnetic materials such as ferromagnets and antiferromagnets. Recently, a large anomalous Hall effect was reported in the noncollinear antiferromagnetic metal NbMnP whose magnetic order is a mixture of the even-parity and the odd-parity magnetic components. Such a magnetic structure is expected to exhibit the anomalous Hall effect and the nonlinear Hall effect from the symmetry breaking of the antiferromagnet ordering. Here, we theoretically investigate the intrinsic anomalous and nonlinear Hall effect of NbMnP induced by the quantum geometry of Bloch band using the first-principles calculation and the Wannier interpolation method. We found that the intrinsic Hall response of NbMnP is predominantly governed by the strongly enhanced Berry curvature and Berry-connection-polarization dipole on a specific mirror plane. These enhanced geometric quantities originate from the spin-orbit-coupling-induced gap openings along the nodal lines. Our results indicate that NbMnP serves as a model system for investigating transport phenomena originating from nodal-lines in parity-mixed antiferromagnets.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.08376v1 公告类型：新 摘要：利用中子和共振 X 射线衍射对粉末和单晶样品研究了 EuTi₂Al₂₀ 的磁性结构，其中磁性 Eu²⁺ 离子形成金刚石网络。传播向量确定为textbfqₘ̊ ₘ=(1,0,0)~r.l.u。从这些衍射测量中。使用不可约表示方法和磁空间群分析检查了具有该传播矢量的空间群 Fdbar3m 中所有可能的磁结构。该磁结构被确定为零磁场下具有磁空间群 P_Inna (#52.320) 或 P_Inn2 (#34.164) 的共线反铁磁结构。在这些磁性结构中，钻石网络上的竞争性磁相互作用会产生挫败感。这些发现为评估金刚石网络磁体中竞争相互作用的作用提供了具体的实验参考，并激发了对相互作用驱动的量子态的进一步研究。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08376v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The magnetic structure of EuTi₂Al₂₀, in which magnetic Eu²⁺ ions form a diamond network, was investigated using neutron and resonant X-ray diffraction on powder and single-crystal samples. The propagation vector was determined to be textbfqₘ̊ ₘ=(1,0,0)~r.l.u. from these diffraction measurements. All possible magnetic structures in the space group Fdbar3m with this propagation vector were examined using the irreducible representation method and magnetic space group analysis. This magnetic structure was identified as a collinear antiferromagnetic structure with the magnetic space group P_Inna (#52.320) or P_Inn2 (#34.164) under zero magnetic field. In these magnetic structure, frustration arises from competing magnetic interactions on the diamond network. These findings provide a concrete experimental reference for assessing the role of competing interactions in diamond-network magnets and motivate further studies of interaction-driven quantum states.

arXiv:2601.08552v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们提出了一种有限温度正则系综行列式量子蒙特卡罗算法，该算法强制执行精确的费米子数并能够稳定模拟相关晶格电子。我们提出了一种稳定的 QR 更新，可将计算复杂度从标准三次缩放 O(β N³⁾ 降低到相对于系统大小 N 的线性缩放 O(β N Nₑ²⁾，其中 Nₑ 是粒子数。这在稀释区域 (Nₑ łl N) 中产生了显着的加速，为强相关低密度相的大规模模拟提供了无偏的途径。我们通过现场哈伯德相互作用在稀电子气上验证了该方法，观察到稀极限内费米子符号问题的抑制。此外，我们将这种方法应用于一维平带系统，其中规范系综允许精确控制填充。我们揭示了半填充状态下低温下的铁磁不稳定性。我们的线性尺度方法为研究稀量子物质中的涌现现象提供了强大的工具。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08552v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We present a finite-temperature canonical-ensemble determinant quantum Monte Carlo algorithm that enforces an exact fermion number and enables stable simulations of correlated lattice electrons. We propose a stabilized QR update that reduces the computational complexity from standard cubic scaling O(β N³⁾ to linear scaling O(β N Nₑ²⁾ with respect to the system size N, where Nₑ is the particle number. This yields a dramatic speedup in dilute regimes (Nₑ łl N), opening unbiased access to large-scale simulations of strongly correlated low-density phases. We validate the method on the dilute electron gas with onsite Hubbard interactions, observing the suppression of the fermion sign problem in the dilute limit. Furthermore, we apply this approach to an one-dimensional flat-band system, where the canonical ensemble allows for precise control over filling. We reveal a ferromagnetic instability at low temperatures in the half-filling regime. Our linear-scaling approach provides a powerful tool for investigating emergent phenomena in dilute quantum matter.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.08613v1 公告类型：新 摘要：双螺旋（DH）纳米线提供了一个研究几何手性对自旋手性影响的平台。它们的三维 (3D) 螺旋结构和可调谐链间耦合能够控制自旋手性，包括稳定拓扑 3D 磁态，例如螺旋畴和畴壁、拓扑杂散场和扩展螺旋涡旋/斯格明子管。到目前为止，对这些和其他 3D 纳米结构的研究通常仅限于大型设施中有限数量的磁显微镜实验。在这里，我们使用暗场磁光克尔效应 (DF-MOKE) 磁力测定法研究外部 3D 磁场下单根 DH 纳米线的反转机制。通过分析 DF-MOKE 信号的角度依赖性，我们使用已建立的畴壁成核和传播模型来拟合反转过程，找到与圆柱形纳米线相似的特征行为。微磁模拟表明，反转过程是螺旋涡管以卷曲方式成核，而叠层X射线磁圆二色性数据表明，这种螺旋涡管状态是通过混合成核-传播过程形成的。这些观察结果提供了由沿纳米线延伸的螺旋涡流管介导的反转的一致微观图像。我们的工作提供了 DH 纳米线磁化反转的全面表征，并证明 DF-MOKE 磁力测量对于探测单个 3D 纳米结构中的反转机制是有效的。这种基于实验室的方法将可进行的实验范围扩展到大型设施之外，从而能够对 3D 纳米几何结构支持的丰富自旋态进行广泛探索。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08613v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Double-helix (DH) nanowires provide a platform to study the influence of geometric chirality on spin chirality. Their three-dimensional (3D) helical architecture and tunable inter-strand coupling enable control of spin chirality, including the stabilization of topological 3D magnetic states such as helical domains and domain walls, topological stray fields, and extended helical vortex/skyrmion tubes. So far, the study of these and other 3D nanostructures is usually confined to a limited number of magnetic microscopy experiments in large facilities. Here, we investigate the reversal mechanism of a single DH nanowire using Dark-Field magneto-optical Kerr effect (DF-MOKE) magnetometry under external 3D magnetic fields. By analyzing the angular dependence of the DF-MOKE signal, we fit the reversal process using established models for domain-wall nucleation and propagation, finding a characteristic behavior similar to that reported for cylindrical nanowires. Micromagnetic simulations indicate that the reversal process goes through nucleation of the helical vortex tube in a curling manner while ptychographic X-ray magnetic circular dichroism data reveal that this helical vortex tube state forms through a mixed nucleation-propagation process. These observations provide a consistent microscopic picture of reversal mediated by a helical vortex tube extending along the nanowire. Our work provides a comprehensive characterization of magnetization reversal in DH nanowires and demonstrates that DF-MOKE magnetometry is effective for probing reversal mechanisms in single 3D nanostructures. This lab-based approach expands the range of accessible experiments beyond large-scale facilities, enabling extensive exploration of the rich spin states supported by 3D nano-geometries.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.08702v1 公告类型：新 摘要：对于由自旋五半离子组成的反铁磁体，如果这些离子形成量子涨落实体（QFE），例如准一维均匀反铁磁链或，则这些离子在有序反铁磁状态下的矩可以显着小于 5 BM （即 1.56 - 4.48 BM）准零自旋反铁磁自旋二聚体。可以合理地假设，这种反铁磁体中的量子涨落越强，其有序矩的减少就越大，但这一假设尚未得到证实，因为量化量子涨落的强度并不是一件简单的事情。在这里，我们通过分析六种反铁磁体表明，涉及 QFE 的局部磁激发可用于量化量子涨落的强度，这些反铁磁体的有序自旋矩显着减少。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08702v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: For antiferromagnets composed of spin five-half ions, the moments of these ions in the ordered antiferromagnetic state can be significantly smaller than 5 BM (i.e., 1.56 - 4.48 BM) if these ions form quantum fluctuating entities (QFEs), for example, quasi one-dimensional uniform antiferromagnetic chains or quasi zero-spin antiferromagnetic spin dimers. It is reasonable to suppose that the stronger the quantum fluctuation in such an antiferromagnet, the greater the reduction in its ordered moment would become, but this supposition has not yet been confirmed because quantifying the strength of quantum fluctuation is not a straightforward matter. Here we show that the local magnetic excitations involving the QFEs can be used to quantify the strength of quantum fluctuation by analyzing six antiferromagnets showing significant reduction in their ordered spin moments.

arXiv:2601.08738v1 公告类型：新 摘要：自旋转移力矩 (STT) 通过电流控制磁化强度，从而实现一系列纳米级自旋电子应用。它们可以通过抵消磁弛豫来破坏平衡磁化状态的稳定。在这里，我们通过 CoFeB 薄膜专用的生长退火协议最大化 STT 效应，使得源自界面和形状的磁各向异性几乎相互抵消。近乎各向同性的磁体能够在与外加磁场相反的方向上实现磁化强度的低电流动态稳定，从而实现卡皮查摆的自旋电子模拟。在中间电流状态下，STT 驱动覆盖整个布洛赫球体的大磁化矢量波动。与随机磁化方向相关联的连续变量可以充当概率计算和神经形态硬件的资源。我们的研究结果将各向同性磁体建立为研究尚未开发的、远离平衡的自旋动力学（包括反磁子学）的平台，对非常规计算范式具有广阔的前景。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08738v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Spin transfer torques (STTs) control magnetisation by electric currents, enabling a range of nano-scale spintronic applications. They can destabilise the equilibrium magnetisation state by counteracting magnetic relaxation. Here, we maximise the STT effect through a dedicated growth-annealing protocol for CoFeB thin films, such that magnetic anisotropies originating from the interface and shape almost cancel each other. The nearly isotropic magnets enable low-current dynamical stabilisation of the magnetisation in the direction opposite to an applied magnetic field, thereby realising a spintronic analogue of the Kapitza pendulum. In an intermediate current regime, the STT drives large magnetisation vector fluctuations that cover the entire Bloch sphere. The continuous variable associated with the stochastic magnetisation direction may serve as a resource for probabilistic computing and neuromorphic hardware. Our results establish isotropic magnets as a platform to study as-yet-uncharted, far-from-equilibrium spin dynamics including anti-magnonics, with promising implications for unconventional computing paradigms.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.08762v1 公告类型：新 摘要：磁相通常通过宏观磁化来识别，但许多有序态，包括反铁磁体和交变磁体，尽管具有不同的局部自旋结构，但仍具有消失的净矩。我们证明，可以通过局部耦合到自旋晶格的单个初级量子位的测量引起的稳态来获得这样的顺序。使用受控的主辅助量子比特协议，我们分析得出稳态 emph编码 在弱耦合状态下呈线性的有符号可观测量中的局部加权交换场。数值模拟证明了反铁磁和交变磁纹理的晶格尺度分辨率以及对短相关噪声的鲁棒性。我们的结果将测量引起的耗散确立为通过微观结构而不是通过全局矩来检测磁序的资源。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08762v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Magnetic phases are commonly identified through macroscopic magnetization, yet many ordered states, including antiferromagnets and altermagnets, possess a vanishing net moment despite distinct local spin structure. We show that such an order can be accessed through the measurement-induced steady state of a single primary qubit locally coupled to a spin lattice. Using a controlled primary-ancillary qubit protocol, we derive analytically that the steady state emphencodes a locally weighted exchange field in a signed observable that is linear in the weak-coupling regime. Numerical simulations demonstrate lattice-scale resolution of antiferromagnetic and altermagnetic textures and robustness against short-correlated noise. Our results establish measurement-induced dissipation as a resource for detecting magnetic order through microscopic structure rather than through global moments.

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08606v1 Announce Type: cross Abstract: We study an open quantum spin chain with non-reciprocal dissipation using a theoretical approach known as time-dependent generalized Gibbs ensemble. 中文摘要

arXiv:2002.01909v3 公告类型：替换 摘要：我们结合密度泛函理论和动态平均场理论，研究了库仑关联效应及其在 12 至 33 GPa 压力下 ǎrepsilon-铁超导性中的作用。我们的结果表明，费米液体行为在 sim1000 K 以下的温度下持续存在。库仑相关性被发现可以显着重整态密度，将峰值到费米能级的距离减小到 0.4 eV，而 DFT 计算中获得的值为 0.75 eV。我们发现显着的反铁磁相关性，伴随着短寿命局部磁矩的形成。我们使用所获得的结果作为构建多能带 Bethe-Salpeter 方程的起点，该方程的特征值表明反铁磁自旋涨落可能导致 ǎrepsilon-Fe 中的超导配对。此外，随着压力的增加，超导不稳定性的趋势变弱，这可以解释超导性在 sim30 GPa 时消失。

English Abstract

arXiv:2002.01909v3 Announce Type: replace Abstract: We study Coulomb correlation effects and their role in superconductivity of ǎrepsilon-iron under pressure from 12 to 33 GPa by using a combination of density functional and dynamical mean-field theory. Our results indicate a persistence of the Fermi-liquid behavior below the temperature sim1000 K. The Coulomb correlations are found to substantially renormalize the density of states, reducing the distance from the peak to the Fermi level to 0.4 eV compared to 0.75 eV obtained in DFT calculations. We find significant antiferromagnetic correlations, which are accompanied by the formation of short-lived local magnetic moments. We use the obtained results as a starting point for construction of the multi-band Bethe-Salpeter equation, which eigenvalues indicate that antiferromagnetic spin fluctuations may result in the superconducting pairing in ǎrepsilon-Fe. Moreover, the tendency to superconducting instability becomes weaker with the increase of pressure, which may explain the disappearance of superconductivity at sim30 GPa.

中文摘要

arXiv:2504.07194v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：竞争自由度、晶体电场和自旋相关性之间的微妙相互作用可能导致 4f 离子基受挫三角晶格反铁磁体中出现奇异的量子态。我们提出了 4f 离子基受挫磁体 Ba4YbReWO12 的晶体结构、热力学和 μ 子自旋弛豫 (μSR) 研究，其中 Yb3+ 离子构成三角形晶格。磁化率没有显示出低至 1.9 K 的自旋冻结或低至 0.4 K 的长程磁有序的任何特征。与逆磁化率数据的低温居里-魏斯拟合揭示了弱的反铁磁交换相互作用，这通过遵循 J1-J2 模型的磁比热数据拟合得到了证实，其中 J1 = -0.197 K 在 Jeff = 1/2 状态之间的最近邻交换相互作用。最低克莱默双峰中的 Yb3+ 时刻。最低的 Kramers 基态双峰与第一激发态分离良好，间隙为 278 K，我们的 μSR 实验证明了这一点，该实验支持在低温下实现 Jeff = 1/2。比热实验未检测到低至 56 mK 的相变。磁比热显示出广泛的最大值 90 mK，表明具有短程自旋相关性的无序基态。低温下相关的磁熵释放与 Jeff = 1/2 状态的预期一致。零场 μSR 测量既没有显示出自旋冻结的特征，也没有显示出相变，至少低至 43 mK。我们的结果表明，在这个 Jeff = 1/2 受抑三角晶格反铁磁体中存在动态、无序的基态。 Ba4RReWO12（R=稀土）提供了一个可行的平台来实现由自旋轨道耦合和挫败产生的有趣的量子态

English Abstract

arXiv:2504.07194v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: The subtle interplay between competing degrees of freedom, crystal electric fields, and spin correlations can lead to exotic quantum states in 4f ion-based frustrated triangular lattice antiferromagnets. We present the crystal structure, thermodynamic and muon spin relaxation (μSR) studies of the 4f ion-based frustrated magnet Ba4YbReWO12, wherein Yb3+ ions constitute a triangular lattice. The magnetic susceptibility does not show any signature of spin freezing down to 1.9 K or long-range magnetic ordering down to 0.4 K. The low-temperature Curie-Weiss fit to the inverse magnetic susceptibility data reveals a weak antiferromagnetic exchange interaction, which is corroborated by the fit of magnetic specific heat data following the J1-J2 model with the nearest neighbor exchange interaction of J1 = -0.197 K between the Jeff = 1/2 states of the Yb3+ moments in the lowest Kramers doublet. The lowest Kramers ground state doublet is well separated from the first excited state with a gap of 278 K, as evidenced by our μSR experiments that support the realization of Jeff = 1/2 at low temperatures. The specific heat experiments do not detect a phase transition down to 56 mK. The magnetic specific heat shows a broad maximum 90 mK suggesting a disordered ground state with short range spin correlations. The associated magnetic entropy release at low temperatures is consistent with that expected for the Jeff = 1/2 state. The zero-field μSR measurements show neither the signature of spin freezing nor a phase transition, at least down to 43 mK. Our results suggest a dynamic, disordered ground state in this Jeff = 1/2 frustrated triangular lattice antiferromagnet. Ba4RReWO12 (R=rare earth) offers a viable platform to realize intriguing quantum states borne out of spin-orbit coupling and frustration

中文摘要

arXiv:2505.20598v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：最近在近磁化 Rashba 型 Pt 约瑟夫森结 (JJ) 中实现的零场、极性可逆超电流整流使得超导逻辑电路和低温存储器应用的发展成为可能。在这里，我们展示了通过超导量子干涉测量法直接探测到的非易失性反常相移 φ₀，为这些 Rashba 型系统中自发时间反转对称性破缺提供了相敏证据。通过用表现出不同（顺）磁化率、自旋轨道耦合强度和电子能带结构的 5d 或 4d 元素层替换 Pt 势垒，我们阐明了邻近效应在控制零场二极管行为中的作用。 Ta (W) JJ 在 2 K 时表现出约 17% (约 5%) 的零场二极管效率，略（显着）低于 Pt JJ。值得注意的是，Ta 和 W JJ 中的二极管极性相对于 Pt JJ 是相反的。结合在高磁敏感性 Pd JJ 中观察到的大零场二极管效率（2 K 时约 15%），这些结果表明，非易失性 φ₀ 以及因此的零场二极管性能可以通过界面磁序和 Rashba 自旋轨道相互作用的邻近工程来调节。

English Abstract

arXiv:2505.20598v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: The recent realization of zero-field, polarity-reversible supercurrent rectification in proximity-magnetized Rashba-type Pt Josephson junctions (JJs) enables the development of superconducting logic circuits and cryogenic memory applications. Here, we demonstrate a non-volatile anomalous phase shift φ₀ directly probed via superconducting quantum interferometry, providing phase-sensitive evidence of spontaneous time-reversal symmetry breaking in these Rashba-type systems. By replacing the Pt barrier with 5d or 4d element layers exhibiting different (para-)magnetic susceptibilities, spin-orbit coupling strengths, and electronic band structures, we elucidate the role of proximity effects in governing zero-field diode behavior. Ta (W) JJs exhibit zero-field diode efficiencies of ~17% (~5%) at 2 K, which are slightly (significantly) lower than those of Pt JJs. Notably, the diode polarity in Ta and W JJs is reversed relative to Pt JJs. Combined with the large zero-field diode efficiency (~15% at 2 K) observed in highly magnetic-susceptible Pd JJs, these results show that non-volatile φ₀ and, consequently, zero-field diode performance can be tuned through proximity engineering of interfacial magnetic ordering and Rashba spin-orbit interaction.

中文摘要

arXiv:2507.17386v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：我们提出了一个简单的理论，解释了最近在可编程量子模拟器上进行的量子粗化和集体动力学实验中的两个中心观察结果 [T. Manovitz et al., Nature 638, 86 (2025)]：随着相变的接近，粗化过程明显加速；以及有序相内淬火后有序参数的持续振荡。我们的理论基于量子模型经典极限中运动方程的哈密顿结构，发现有序相内部已经加速，随后随着畴壁张力在接近临界线时消失而减速。此外，在阶次参数场的平均场处理中捕获振荡。对于有序相内的猝灭，初始平均场中微小的空间变化波动会导致显着的长期效应，其中系统动态地破坏其长程有序并必须粗化以重新建立它。我们将这种现象称为 emph对称性重新破缺，因为由此产生的后期磁化强度可能具有与初始磁化强度相反的符号。

English Abstract

arXiv:2507.17386v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: We present a simple theory accounting for two central observations in a recent experiment on quantum coarsening and collective dynamics on a programmable quantum simulator [T. Manovitz et al., Nature 638, 86 (2025)]: an apparent speeding up of the coarsening process as the phase transition is approached; and persistent oscillations of the order parameter after quenches within the ordered phase. Our theory, based on the Hamiltonian structure of the equations of motion in the classical limit of the quantum model, finds a speeding up already deep within the ordered phase, with subsequent slowing down as the domain wall tension vanishes upon approaching the critical line. Further, the oscillations are captured within a mean-field treatment of the order parameter field. For quenches within the ordered phase, small spatially-varying fluctuations in the initial mean-field lead to a remarkable long-time effect, wherein the system dynamically destroys its long-range order and has to coarsen to re-establish it. We term this phenomenon emphsymmetry re-breaking, as the resulting late-time magnetization can have a sign opposite to the initial magnetization.

English Abstract

arXiv:2509.17633v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Two ternary liquid crystalline mixtures are formulated and investigated by differential scanning calorimetry, polarizing optical microscopy, X-ray diffraction, and broadband dielectric spectroscopy. Paraelectric smectic A*, ferroelectric smectic C*, and antiferroelectric smectic C_A* phases are detected. The glass of the smectic C_A* phase is formed at moderate cooling rates. Vitrification prevents the approaching transition to a hexatic smectic phase. One mixture shows a strong thermochromic effect in the smectic C_A* phase and selectively reflects blue light in the glassy state. Both mixtures reflect either green or red light in the smectic C* phase, depending on temperature treatment: whether the sample is cooled or heated, or at which rate the temperature changes.

中文摘要

arXiv:2510.07465v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：我们报道了通过高温离轴射频磁控溅射外延生长纳米厚的铋取代钇铁石榴石（BiYIG）薄膜。我们展示了通过调整各种（111）取向石榴石基板上的溅射参数和外延应变来精确控制磁性。 BiYIG 薄膜与基底的晶格失配高达 -0.80%，但仍保持完全应变，厚度可达 60nm，从而保持高结晶质量。透射电子显微镜和能量色散 X 射线光谱证实了 BiYIG/衬底界面的相干外延生长、不存在缺陷以及有限的相互扩散。在 BiYIG 中改变 -0.80% 和 +0.56% 之间的拉伸或压缩应变，可以通过磁弹性耦合精确补偿总磁各向异性。溅射 BiYIG 薄膜的有效磁各向异性可以通过离轴沉积角度和生长过程中的氧气流量进一步调节，这决定了阳离子化学计量。在优化的生长条件下，即使厚度低至 10nm，也能可靠地获得 10GHz 下 1mT 的铁磁共振 (FMR) 线宽。我们还报告了在抗磁性衬底钇钪镓石榴石上生长的超薄（2-5 nm）BiYIG 薄膜中的小 FMR 线宽。这些发现凸显了低阻尼、应变工程纳米厚 BiYIG 薄膜在自旋轨道电子和磁振子器件中实现先进功能的前景。具体来说，磁各向异性补偿和低阻尼使得大锥角磁化动力学不受磁振子-磁振子非线性散射的影响。

English Abstract

arXiv:2510.07465v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: We report on the epitaxial growth of nm-thick films of bismuth-substituted yttrium iron garnet (BiYIG) by high-temperature off-axis radio-frequency magnetron sputtering. We demonstrate accurate control of the magnetic properties by tuning of the sputtering parameters and epitaxial strain on various (111)-oriented garnet substrates. BiYIG films with up to -0.80% lattice mismatch with the substrate remain fully strained up to 60~nm-thick, maintaining a high crystalline quality. Transmission electron microscopy and energy-dispersive X-ray spectroscopy confirm coherent epitaxial growth, the absence of defects, and limited interdiffusion at the BiYIG/substrate interface. Varying the tensile or compressive strain between -0.80% and +0.56% in BiYIG allows for accurate compensation of the total magnetic anisotropy through magneto-elastic coupling. The effective magnetic anisotropy of sputtered BiYIG films can be further tuned via the off-axis deposition angle and the oxygen flow during growth, which determine the cation stoichiometry. Under optimized growth conditions, a ferromagnetic resonance (FMR) linewidth of 1~mT at 10~GHz is reliably obtained even for thicknesses as low as 10~nm. We also report small FMR linewidths in ultrathin (2-5~nm) BiYIG films grown on diamagnetic substrate yttrium scandium gallium garnet. These findings highlight the promise of low-damping, strain-engineered nm-thick BiYIG films for implementing advanced functionalities in spin-orbitronic and magnonic devices. Specifically, the magnetic-anisotropy compensation and low damping enable large cone-angle magnetization dynamics immune to magnon-magnon nonlinear scattering.

中文摘要

arXiv:2510.23376v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：利用随机级数展开量子蒙特卡罗和密度矩阵重整化群方法，我们研究了二维方六边形（SHO）晶格上 S=1/2 海森堡模型的基态相图。该模型包含最近邻相互作用 J₁（六边形内相互作用）和 J₂（六边形间），以及沿 x 方向选定的第三邻相互作用 J₃。我们在参数体系 0<łambda₁₌J₂/J₁<4, 0<łambda₂₌J₃/J₁<4 中确定了五个不同的相：一个 Néel 反铁磁相、两个二聚体相（正交和梯形交错二聚体）、一个六边形单重态相，以及值得注意的一个类 Haldane 对称保护拓扑 (SPT) 相。类霍尔丹相的拓扑性质通过开放边界条件下基态能量的简并性和纠缠谱的双重简并性得到证实。使用自旋刚度和粘合剂累积量的有限尺寸缩放来准确确定相边界。数据崩溃分析表明，所有从非磁性相到反铁磁性相的转变都属于三维 O(3) 海森堡普适性类。此外，我们还研究了 SPT 相对其他相互作用的稳健性，例如实验材料中可能出现的相互作用。我们的工作建立了一个全面的理论框架来理解 SHO 晶格的磁相和拓扑相。

English Abstract

arXiv:2510.23376v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Using stochastic series expansion quantum Monte Carlo and density matrix renormalization group methods, we investigate the ground-state phase diagram of the S=1/2 Heisenberg model on the two-dimensional square-hexagon-octagon (SHO) lattice. The model incorporates nearest-neighbor interactions J₁ (intrahexagon interaction) and J₂ (interhexagon), as well as a selected third-neighbor interaction J₃ along the x direction. We identify five distinct phases in the parameter regime 0<łambda₁₌J₂/J₁<4, 0<łambda₂₌J₃/J₁<4: a Néel antiferromagentic phase, two dimer phases (orthogonal and ladder staggered dimers), a hexagon singlet phase, and notably a Haldane-like symmetry-protected topological (SPT) phase. The topological nature of the Haldane-like phase is confirmed by the degeneracy of the ground-state energy under open boundary conditions and the twofold degeneracy of the entanglement spectrum. Phase boundaries are accurately determined using finite-size scaling of the spin stiffness and Binder cumulant. Data collapse analysis reveals that all transitions from nonmagnetic phases to the antiferromagnetic phase belong to the three-dimensional O(3) Heisenberg universality class. In addition, we investigate the robustness of the SPT phase to other interactions, such as those that could arise in experimental materials. Our work establishes a comprehensive theoretical framework for understanding magnetic and topological phases on the SHO lattice.

中文摘要

arXiv:2511.20287v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：电流驱动的畴壁和斯格明子运动是非易失性磁存储器件操作的核心。赛道存储器需要足够高的电流密度才能产生超过 50 m/s 的速度，但这种条件也会增强自旋电流噪声。我们开发了一个基于随机蒂勒方程的理论框架来分析平衡（热）和非平衡（自旋流）涨落对斯格明子动力学的影响。通过这种方法，我们得出了量化两个噪声源下的随机运动的扩散系数和均方位移。微磁模拟和分析结果表明，在直至室温的典型跑道结构中，自旋电流噪声主导着斯格明子动力学。我们进一步解决了首次通过时间问题，获得了赛道上和整个赛道的平均首次通过时间及其标准差。这些结果量化了随机位移如何影响斯格明子传播和检测，从而深入了解高速赛道存储设备中的误差源。

English Abstract

arXiv:2511.20287v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Current-driven motion of domain walls and skyrmions is central to the operation of non-volatile magnetic memory devices. Racetrack memory requires current densities high enough to generate velocities above 50 m/s, but such conditions also enhance spin-current noise. We develop a theoretical framework based on the stochastic Thiele equation to analyze the effects of equilibrium (thermal) and nonequilibrium (spin-current) fluctuations on skyrmion dynamics. From this approach, we derive diffusion coefficients and mean-squared displacements that quantify stochastic motion under both noise sources. Micromagnetic simulations and analytical results demonstrate that spin-current noise dominates skyrmion dynamics in typical racetrack structures up to room temperature. We further address the first-passage-time problem, obtaining the mean first-passage time and its standard deviation along and across the racetrack. These results quantify how random displacements affect skyrmion propagation and detection, providing insights into error sources in high-speed racetrack memory devices.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.08059v1 公告类型：新 摘要：磁性纳米结构的高分辨率成像对于理解基本自旋现象和设计先进器件至关重要。三维 (3D) 纳米磁性的最新发展凸显了对能够以高灵敏度捕获弯曲或倾斜表面上的磁性结构的成像技术的日益增长的需求。尽管广泛用作磁化态成像的强大技术，但传统磁光克尔效应 (MOKE) 显微镜由于其景深 (DOF) 较浅，在测量非平面系统方面面临着固有的局限性。在这里，我们提出了一种扩展景深的 MOKE 成像方法，将离焦扫描与基于图像拼接的重建相结合，以获得跨非平面样品几何形状的清晰且分辨率良好的磁域图像。该方法在本研究中特意倾斜的垂直和面内磁化薄膜上进行了验证，从而能够对磁畴形态和检测灵敏度进行定量分析。这种实验室可用的技术为 3D 磁成像提供了一种快速且通用的途径，补充了基于 X 射线的大规模方法，并为研究具有倾斜或弯曲 3D 几何形状的非平面磁性样品提供了实用工具。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.08059v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: High-resolution imaging of magnetic nanostructures is essential for understanding fundamental spin phenomena and designing advanced devices. Recent developments in three-dimensional (3D) nanomagnetism have highlighted the growing need for imaging techniques that can capture magnetic structures across curved or tilted surfaces with high sensitivity. Though widely used as a powerful technique for imaging magnetization states, conventional magneto-optical Kerr effect (MOKE) microscopy faces inherent limitations in measuring non-planar systems due to its shallow depth of field (DOF). Here, we present an extended depth of field MOKE imaging approach, combining through-focus scanning with image-stitching-based reconstruction, to obtain sharp and well-resolved magnetic domain images across non-planar sample geometries. The method is validated on both perpendicularly and in-plane magnetized films tilted on purpose for this study, enabling quantitative analysis of domain morphology and detection sensitivity. This laboratory-accessible technique provides a fast and versatile route for 3D magnetic imaging, complementing large-scale X-ray-based methods and offering a practical tool for investigating non-planar magnetic samples with tilted or curved 3D geometries.

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06267v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Nanosized hafnia-zirconia HfxZr1-xO2 in the form of thin films, multilayers and heterostructures are indispensable silicon-compatible ferroelectric materials for advanced electronic memories and logic devices. The distinctive feature of nanoscale hafnia-zirconia are the critical sizes of ferroelectricity appearance, whereas the critical sizes of ferroelectricity disappearance exist in other ferroelectrics. Using the Landau-Ginzburg-Devonshire free energy functional with higher powers, trilinear and biquadratic couplings of polar, nonpolar and antipolar order parameters, we calculated analytically the strain-dependent critical sizes of the ferroelectricity appearance and disappearance, analyzed how the size effect and mismatch strains influence the phase diagrams and polarization switching barrier in epitaxial HfO2 thin films and nano-islands with the out-of-plane spontaneous polarization. We have shown that the critical thickness/height of out-of-plane spontaneous polarization disappearance is determined by the size dependence of the depolarization field and correlation effects. The critical thickness/height of the ferroelectricity appearance is determined by the size dependence of the effective mismatch strain considering possible appearance of misfit dislocations and lateral relaxion of strains. Derived analytical expressions can be generalized for HfxZr1-xO2 solid solutions, providing that corresponding parameters of the free energy are known from the first principles calculations.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.06274v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们利用自旋扭矩铁磁共振方法研究了居里温度 Tₘ̊ C 为 310 K 的范德华 (vdW) 铁磁体 Fe₅GeTe₂ (FGT) 中的自旋霍尔效应 (SHE)。与铁磁相的出现同步，导致异常霍尔效应 (AHE)，在 Tₘ̊ C 以下观察到 SHE 的显着增强。另一方面，SHE 显示出与 AHE 不同的温度依赖性：与反常霍尔电导率不同，有效自旋霍尔电导率随着温度的降低而明显增强，反映了伴随着 FGT 复杂磁序的能带结构的变化。这些结果提供了对磁性材料中的 SHE 的深入理解，为基于 vdW 材料的自旋电子器件的新功能开辟了一条新途径。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06274v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We investigate the spin Hall effect (SHE) in a van der Waals (vdW) ferromagnet Fe₅GeTe₂ (FGT) with a Curie temperature Tₘ̊ C of 310 K utilizing the spin-torque ferromagnetic resonance method. In synchronization with the emergence of the ferromagnetic phase resulting in the anomalous Hall effect (AHE), a noticeable enhancement in the SHE was observed below Tₘ̊ C. On the other hand, the SHE shows a different temperature dependence from the AHE: the effective spin Hall conductivity is clearly enhanced with decreasing temperature unlike the anomalous Hall conductivity, reflecting the variation of band-structure accompanied by the complicated magnetic ordering of the FGT. The results provide a deep understanding of the SHE in magnetic materials to open a new route for novel functionalities in vdW materials-based spintronic devices.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.06365v1 公告类型：新 摘要：相变在现代凝聚态物理及其应用中无处不在。在固体中，相变通常通过非平衡条件下的成核和生长而发生。在恒定的外部条件下，e.g.，恒定的加热温度和压力，成核和生长动力学通常被认为是空间和时间独立的。在这里，原位布拉格X射线光子相关光谱（XPCS）揭示了La₀.₇Sr₀.₃CoO₃ (LSCO)薄膜中钙钛矿到褐针石拓扑相变的纳米级空间和动力学异质性，在持续还原条件下持续数小时。具体来说，与域生长相关的时间尺度保持稳定，相应的域壁速度为 v_d = 6 ± 0.5 ×10⁻⁴ nm/s (2 ± 0.2 nm/h)，而与温度驱动的域脱钉相关的较慢的时间尺度，导致遵循指数 -2.2 ± 0.5 的老化幂律的时间尺度的加速动力学。实验表明，布拉格 XPCS 是研究相变纳米级动力学的强大工具。这些结果与相变器件的相工程相关，因为它们表明，与磁畴和磁畴壁运动相关的纳米级动力学可以随着时间不断演化和加速，甚至在相变开始后几个小时内，对电性能有潜在的影响。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06365v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Phase transitions are omnipresent in modern condensed matter physics and its applications. In solids, phase transformations typically occur by nucleation and growth under non-equilibrium conditions. Under constant external conditions, e.g., constant heating temperature and pressure, the nucleation and growth dynamics are often thought of as spatially and temporally independent. Here, in-situ Bragg X-ray photon correlation spectroscopy (XPCS) reveals nanoscale spatial and dynamical heterogeneity in the perovskite to brownmillerite topotactic phase transformation in La₀.₇Sr₀.₃CoO₃ (LSCO) thin films under constant reducing conditions over a time-span of multiple hours. Specifically, a timescale associated with domain growth remains stable, with a corresponding domain wall speed of v_d = 6 ± 0.5 ×10⁻⁴ nm/s (2 ± 0.2 nm/h), while a slower timescale, associated with temperature driven de-pinning of domains, leads to accelerating dynamics with timescales following an aging power law with exponent -2.2 ± 0.5. The experiment demonstrates that Bragg XPCS is a powerful tool to study nanoscale dynamics in phase transformations. The results are relevant for phase engineering of phase-change devices, as they show that nanoscale dynamics, linked to domain and domain-wall motion, can continuously evolve and speed up with time, even hours after the initiation of the phase transformation, with potential repercussions on electrical performance.

arXiv:2601.06422v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们使用带有哈伯德 U 校正的自旋极化第一性原理密度泛函理论 (DFT) 研究反铁磁 (AFM) 亚铬酸镧 (LaCrO₃₎、锰酸镧 (LaMnO₃₎ 和铁氧体镧 (LaFeO₃₎ 的自旋相关电子态。计算了 15 种不同 AFM 结构的能带结构。经验证，对于这些结构，存在一个非常简单的规则来识别哪个波数 k 在能带结构中表现出自旋分裂或简并性。该规则使用将上自旋原子映射到下自旋原子的对称运算。对于最稳定实验结构的最稳定自旋构型而言，产生的自旋分裂非常小。我们讨论了这种特性的一个看似合理的好处，即在电极应用中自旋电流的方向无关性。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06422v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We investigate spin-dependent electronic states of antiferromagnetic (AFM) lanthanum chromite (LaCrO₃₎, lanthanum manganite (LaMnO₃₎, and lanthanum ferrite (LaFeO₃₎ using spin-polarized first-principles density functional theory (DFT) with Hubbard U correction. The band structures are calculated for 15 types of their different AFM structures. It is verified for these structures that there is a very simple rule to identify which wave number k exhibits spin splitting or degeneracy in the band structure. This rule uses the symmetry operations that map the up-spin atoms onto the down-spin atoms. The resulting spin splitting is very small for the most stable spin configuration of the most stable experimental structure. We discuss a plausible benefit of this characteristic, i.e., the direction-independence of the spin current, in electrode applications.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.06440v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们提出了由具有强轨道选择性层间杂化的过渡金属双层系统驱动的四分之一孔填充双轨道双层哈伯德模型的低能物理理论研究。通过明确处理分子轨道基础内 dz2 轨道的强层间键合并投影出高能电子态，我们推导了一个低能有效的 Kugel-Khomskii 哈密顿量，描述了电子自旋和涌现层赝自旋自由度之间的相互作用。我们绘制了丰富的基态相图，具有不同的自旋和电荷有序态。这些包括具有层交错电荷密度的传统铁磁和反铁磁相、以自发层间量子相干为特征的层相干相，以及具有隐藏复合自旋层序的新型最大自旋层纠缠相。我们证明，这种奇异的隐藏有序相源于 O(4) 对称性自发破缺到 O(3)，表现出具有三种纠缠无间隙戈德斯通模式的独特激发光谱。我们的研究结果揭示了在强相关双层系统中实现复合纠缠的几何驱动机制，并提供了与双层镍酸盐超导体和其他多组分相关材料相关的具体理论框架。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06440v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We present a theoretical study of the low-energy physics of a quarter-hole-filled two-orbital bilayer Hubbard model motivated by transition-metal bilayer systems with strong orbital-selective interlayer hybridization. By explicitly treating the strong interlayer bonding of dz2 orbitals within a molecular orbital basis and projecting out high-energy electronic states, we derive a low-energy effective Kugel-Khomskii Hamiltonian describing the interplay between electron spin and emergent layer pseudospin degrees of freedom. We map out a rich ground state phase diagram featuring diverse spin and charge ordered states. These include conventional ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic phases with layer staggered charge densities, a layer-coherent phase characterized by spontaneous interlayer quantum coherence, and a novel maximally spin-layer-entangled phase with a hidden composite spin-layer order. We show that this exotic hidden ordered phase arises from the spontaneous breaking of an emergent O(4) symmetry down to a O(3), manifesting a unique excitation spectrum with three entangled gapless Goldstone modes. Our results uncover a geometrically driven mechanism for realizing composite entanglement in strongly correlated bilayer systems and provide a concrete theoretical framework relevant to bilayer nickelate superconductors and other multi-component correlated materials.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.06511v1 公告类型：新 摘要：Altermagnet (AM) 是最近发现的一类共线磁体，由于其零净磁化强度和自旋分裂能带的独特组合而引起了广泛关注，导致了各种新颖的物理现象。使用数值精确的晶格蒙特卡罗模拟，我们研究了 Ising-Kondo 晶格模型中的类 AM 相，该模型通常用于描述重费米子材料。通过纳入由交变磁性候选材料中非磁性原子的影响产生的交替次近邻跳跃（NNNH）项，我们的结果揭示了类 AM 态的关键特征，包括自旋分裂准粒子带和光谱函数，并证明 d 波 AM 在广泛的相互作用强度、掺杂水平、NNNH 振幅和温度范围内保持稳定，突出了其鲁棒性。此外，通过非磁性杂质效应的分析，我们进一步证实了AM相的d波对称性。这些发现为探索 f 电子化合物中的类 AM 相奠定了坚实的理论基础，为未来研究其奇异的磁和电子特性铺平了道路。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06511v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Altermagnet (AM), a recently identified class of collinear magnet, has garnered significant attention due to its unique combination of zero net magnetization and spin-split energy bands, leading to a variety of novel physical phenomena. Using numerically exact lattice Monte Carlo simulations, we investigate AM-like phases within the Ising-Kondo lattice model which is commonly employed to describe heavy-fermion materials. By incorporating an alternating next-nearest-neighbor hopping (NNNH) term, which arises from the influence of non-magnetic atoms in altermagnetic candidate materials, our results reveal key signatures of AM-like states, including spin-splitting quasiparticle bands and spectral functions, and demonstrate that d-wave AM remains stable across a broad range of interaction strengths, doping levels, NNNH amplitudes and temperatures, highlighting its robustness. Furthermore, through an analysis of non-magnetic impurity effects, we further confirm the d-wave symmetry of the AM phase. These findings establish a solid theoretical foundation for exploring AM-like phases in f-electron compounds, paving the way for future investigations into their exotic magnetic and electronic properties.

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06585v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Magnetite ferrite (Fe3O4) nanoparticles have attracted considerable interest due to their tunable physico-chemical properties and relevance in functional materials. In this work, uncoated Fe3O4 nanoparticles and surface-modified Fe3O4 nanoparticles coated with polyethylene glycol (PEG-6000) and citric acid (CA) were synthesized via a chemical co-precipitation method. The effect of surface functionalization on the structural, spectroscopic, magnetic, and colloidal properties of the nanoparticles was systematically investigated. X-ray diffraction analysis confirmed the formation of phase-pure Fe3O4 with an inverse spinel structure for all the samples. Fourier transform infrared and Raman spectroscopy verified successful surface modification while preserving the Fe-O framework of the magnetite core. Dynamic light scattering and zeta potential measurements indicated improved dispersion and colloidal stability for the surface-modified nanoparticles. Magnetization studies performed at room temperature revealed superparamagnetic behaviour for all samples, accompanied by a coating-dependent reduction in saturation magnetization. Overall, the results emphasize the critical role of surface chemistry in tailoring the physicochemical, magnetic, and colloidal behaviour of Fe3O4 nanoparticles. Keywords: Fe3O4 nanoparticles, PEG, Citric acid, Co-precipitation, Surface functionalization, Zeta potential, Colloidal stability, Magnetic properties

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.06632v1 公告类型：新 摘要：随着计算能力需求的持续增长，超导电子器件提供了通过提高数字逻辑和存储器的能源效率来降低功耗的机会。扩展这项技术的一个关键里程碑是高效超导存储器的开发。此类设备应该是非易失性的，可扩展至高集成密度和存储容量，能够实现快速、低功耗的读写操作，并且与数字逻辑兼容。我们提出了一个通用设备平台来开发这种非易失性存储设备，该设备由封装在两个铁磁绝缘体（FI）之间的交换耦合超薄超导体组成。超导交换耦合可通过 FI 磁化强度之间的相对排列进行调节，从而实现超导性的开启和关闭。我们利用这种机制来创建超导非易失性存储器，其中使用热辅助磁记录实现单单元写入，并解释它如何成为最先进的超导存储器的竞争者。此外，在低于临界温度时，存储元件表现出明显的不可逆性，零磁场超导二极管效率超过±60%，显示了所提出的超导计算设备的多功能性。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06632v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: As computing power demands continue to grow, superconducting electronics present an opportunity to reduce power consumption by increasing the energy efficiency of digital logic and memory. A key milestone for scaling this technology is the development of efficient superconducting memories. Such devices should be nonvolatile, scalable to high integration density and memory capacity, enable fast and low-power reading and writing operations, and be compatible with the digital logic. We present a versatile device platform to develop such nonvolatile memory devices consisting of an exchange-coupled ultra-thin superconductor encapsulated between two ferromagnetic insulators (FIs). The superconducting exchange coupling, which is tuneable by the relative alignment between the FI magnetizations, enables the switching of superconductivity on and off. We exploit this mechanism to create a superconducting nonvolatile memory where single-cell writing is realized using heat-assisted magnetic recording, and explain how it can become a contender for state-of-the-art superconducting memories. Furthermore, below their critical temperatures, the memory elements show a marked nonreciprocity, with zero magnetic field superconducting diode efficiencies exceeding ±60%, showing the versatility of the proposed devices for superconducting computing.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.06646v1 公告类型：新 摘要：反铁磁体 (AFM) 有望在数字逻辑中得到应用。然而，切换 AFM 域具有挑战性，因为磁场不耦合到体反铁磁有序参数。在这里，我们表明，在许多情况下，磁场驱动的 AFM 域切换可以通过表面磁交换的一般减少来实现。我们使用统计力学和蒙特卡罗模拟来证明，顶部和底部表面力矩之间磁交换的不等价性，再加上表面自旋增强的磁化率，可以根据磁场斜坡方向确定性地选择反铁磁域。我们进一步表明，这种机制为范德华原子力显微镜 MnBi₂Te₄ 磁光响应中磁滞现象的实验观察提供了自然的解释。我们的研究结果强调了表面自旋在反铁磁体对磁场的响应中的关键作用。此外，我们的结果表明，通过纯磁性手段进行的反铁磁畴选择可能是比之前假设的更常见且实验上容易实现的现象。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06646v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Antiferromagnets (AFMs) hold promise for applications in digital logic. However, switching AFM domains is challenging, as magnetic fields do not couple to the bulk antiferromagnetic order parameter. Here we show that magnetic-field-driven switching of AFM domains can in many cases be enabled by a generic reduction of magnetic exchange at surfaces. We use statistical mechanics and Monte Carlo simulations to demonstrate that an inequivalence in magnetic exchange between top and bottom surface moments, combined with the enhanced magnetic susceptibility of surface spins, can enable deterministic selection of antiferromagnetic domains depending on the magnetic-field ramping direction. We further show that this mechanism provides a natural interpretation for experimental observations of hysteresis in magneto-optical response of the van der Waals AFM MnBi₂Te₄. Our findings highlight the critical role of surface spins in responses of antiferromagnets to magnetic fields. Furthermore, our results suggest that antiferromagnetic domain selection via purely magnetic means may be a more common and experimentally accessible phenomenon than previously assumed.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.06691v1 公告类型：新 摘要：磁弹性特性在工业应用中发挥着至关重要的作用。尽管隐藏在纯磁或弹性行为背后，但磁弹性发生在传感器、声学执行器或快速响应传感器等各种设备中。在这项工作中，我们研究了高阶项对各向异性磁致伸缩行为的影响。关于从头计算，各向异性磁致伸缩可以与磁晶能量的应变依赖性相关。通常，描述仅限于磁致弹性能的线性应变依赖性。在这里，我们推导出 bcc 和 fcc 晶体结构的应变中的高阶项。使用简单的参数化，我们表明对于所研究的立方系统，高阶应变项的影响可以忽略不计。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06691v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Magnetoelastic properties play a vital role in industrial applications. Despite being hidden behind either purely magnetic or elastic behavior, magnetoelasticity takes place in a wide range of devices as transducers, acoustic actuators, or fast response sensors. In this work, we inspect the impact of higher-order terms on the anisotropic magnetostriction behavior. Regarding ab-initio calculations, the anisotropic magnetostriction can be related to the strain dependence of the magnetocrystaline energy. Commonly, the description is restricted to a linear strain dependence in the magnetoelastic energy. Here, we derive higher-order terms in strain for bcc and fcc crystal structures. Using a simple parametrization, we show that the influence of the higher-order strain terms is negligible for the studied cubic systems.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.06735v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们系统地研究了有限填充的方晶格 Hubbard 模型中有限动量 Fulde-Ferrell-Larkin-Ovchinnikov (FFLO) 超导性的出现，由 dₓy 波或 dₓ²-y² 波交变磁序在现场存在的情况下驱动s波有吸引力的互动。我们的研究将超导相的平均场计算与正常状态的配对不稳定性分析相结合，并将单粒子色散关系中的次近邻跳跃纳入其中。我们证明了两种类型的交变磁力对 FFLO 状态的稳定具有明显不同的影响。具体来说，dₓy波交变磁力在低填充量下在广泛的参数范围内支持FFLO超导性，而dₓ²-y²波交变磁力仅在高填充量下在窄范围内诱导FFLO配对。此外，我们发现态密度中范霍夫奇点的存在往往会抑制 FFLO 超导性。这些发现可能为具有更复杂电子结构的真实材料中交变磁感应的 FFLO 态的实验探索提供指导。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06735v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We systematically investigate the emergence of finite-momentum Fulde-Ferrell-Larkin-Ovchinnikov (FFLO) superconductivity in a square lattice Hubbard model with finite filling, driven by either dₓy-wave or dₓ²-y²-wave altermagnetic order in the presence of on-site s-wave attractive interactions. Our study combines mean-field calculation in the superconducting phase with pairing instability analysis of the normal state, incorporating the next-nearest-neighbor hopping in the single-particle dispersion relation. We demonstrate that the two types of altermagnetism have markedly different impacts on the stabilization of FFLO states. Specifically, dₓy-wave altermagnetism supports FFLO superconductivity over a broad parameter regime at low fillings, whereas dₓ²-y²-wave altermagnetism only induces FFLO pairing in a narrow range at high fillings. Furthermore, we find that the presence of a Van Hove singularity in the density of states tends to suppress FFLO superconductivity. These findings may provide guidance for experimental exploration of altermagnetism-induced FFLO states in real materials with more complex electronic structures.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.06738v1 公告类型：新 摘要：磁性斯格明子是局部磁性结构，由于其拓扑性质，它可以随着时间的推移保持其形状和稳定性。最近的理论和实验进展为理解具有可忽略的净磁化强度和超快动力学特征的磁性斯格明子奠定了基础。值得注意的是，在具有交变磁性的材料中出现的斯格明子，一种以提高克莱默简并性为特征的新型磁相，迄今为止尚未有报道。在这项研究中，我们证明了 BiFeO3（一种以其铁电性和磁性之间的强耦合而闻名的多铁性材料）可以在室温下在抗阻尼自旋轨道扭矩下从自旋摆线转变为尼尔型斯格明子。引人注目的是，BiFeO3 斯格明子内的交变磁自旋分裂可以通过施加电场来逆转，这通过圆形光电效应揭示。这种具有中性拓扑电荷的准粒子对于多种应用具有巨大的前景，最值得注意的是，能够开发具有低功耗和磁电可控性的非常规计算系统。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06738v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Magnetic skyrmions are localized magnetic structures that retain their shape and stability over time, thanks to their topological nature. Recent theoretical and experimental progress has laid the groundwork for understanding magnetic skyrmions characterized by negligible net magnetization and ultrafast dynamics. Notably, skyrmions emerging in materials with altermagnetism, a novel magnetic phase featuring lifted Kramers degeneracy-have remained unreported until now. In this study, we demonstrate that BiFeO3, a multiferroic renowned for its strong coupling between ferroelectricity and magnetism, can transit from a spin cycloid to a Neel-type skyrmion under antidamping spin-orbit torque at room temperature. Strikingly, the altermagnetic spin splitting within BiFeO3 skyrmion can be reversed through the application of an electric field, revealed via the Circular photogalvanic effect. This quasiparticle, which possesses a neutral topological charge, holds substantial promise for diverse applications-most notably, enabling the development of unconventional computing systems with low power consumption and magnetoelectric controllability.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.06791v1 公告类型：新 摘要：最近，交变磁学话题引起了极大的关注，RuO2 已被证明是最有前途的交变磁候选材料之一。然而，对于RuO2中是否存在磁序仍存在争议。在这项工作中，我们采用 X 射线线性二色性 (XLD)（一种广泛使用的表征反铁磁体的技术），结合光电电子显微镜和多重散射计算，为外延 RuO2 薄膜中不存在磁序提供了明确的证据。观察到的 XLD 信号几乎不随温度变化，并且与冷却场方向无关，这与多重散射计算预测的大量与磁序相关的 XLD 信号形成鲜明对比。这一发现强烈表明 RuO2 的非磁性起源。此外，我们在不同表面取向的 TiO2 基底上生长的 RuO2 薄膜中，在 Ru M3 和 O K 边缘观察到明显不同的 XLD 信号，这可归因于低对称性晶体场。这些结果明确证明了 RuO2 中不存在磁序，并将 XLD 测量确立为探测低对称性磁性材料的可靠技术。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06791v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Recently, the topic of altermagnetism has attracted tremendous attention and RuO2 have been demonstrated to be one of the most promising altermagnetic candidates. However, disputes still remain on the existence of magnetic order in RuO2. Here in this work, we employ X-ray linear dichroism (XLD), a widely utilized technique for characterizing antiferromagnets, in conjunction with photoemission electron microscopy and multiple scattering calculation to provide clear evidence of the absence of magnetic order in epitaxial RuO2 films. The observed XLD signal is nearly invariant with temperature and independent on cooling field direction, in stark contrast to the substantial magnetic order-related XLD signal predicted by multiple scattering calculation. This finding strongly suggests a nonmagnetic origin for RuO2. Furthermore, we observed significantly distinct XLD signals at the Ru M3 and O K edges in RuO2 films grown on TiO2 substrate with different surface orientations, which can be attributed to the low-symmetry crystal field. These results unequivocally demonstrate the absence of magnetic order in RuO2 and establishes XLD measurement as a robust technique for probing the low-symmetry magnetic materials.

arXiv:2601.06936v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们提出了一种用于 spin-1 系统的统一几何方法，该方法连接了看似不同的几何表示，例如向列指向矢、笛卡尔表示和马约拉纳恒星表示。从两个可区分的自旋 1/2 粒子的乘积态开始，我们提供了一种捕获关键几何信息的直接方法。这种观点揭示了子空间投影和几何约束之间的基本相互作用。这种方法有效地将磁孤子映射到扭结模型上，使我们能够推导出它们的运动方程，这是传统方法不易完成的任务。这种简化的动力学描述表明，谐波陷阱中这些孤子的新颖转变对应于基础几何结构中扭结和倾角结构之间的基本变换。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.06936v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We present a unified geometric approach for spin-1 systems that connects seemingly distinct geometric representations such as the nematic director, the Cartesian representation and the Majorana stellar representation. This simplified dynamical description reveals that the novel transition of these solitons in a harmonic trap corresponds to a fundamental transformation between kink and dip structures in the underlying geometry.

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.07083v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Engineering sublattice imbalance within the unit cell of bottom-up synthesized graphene nanoribbons (GNRs) represents a versatile tool for realizing custom-tailored quantum nanomaterials. The interaction between low-energy zero-modes (ZMs) not only contributes to frontier bands but can form the basis for magnetically ordered phases. Here, we present the bottom-up synthesis of a non-centrosymmetric GNR that places all ZMs on the majority sublattice sites. Scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy reveal that strong electron-electron correlation drives the system into a ferromagnetically ordered insulating ground state featuring a sizeable band gap of Eg ~ 1.2 eV. At higher temperatures, a chemical transformation induces an insulator-to-metal transition that quenches the ferro-magnetic order. Tight-binding (TB) and first-principles density functional theory calculations corroborate our experimental observations. This work showcases how control over molecular symmetry, sublattice polarization, and ZM hybridization in bottom-up synthesized nanographenes can open a path to the exploration of many-body physics in rationally designed quantum materials.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.07115v1 公告类型：新 摘要：磁性纳米薄膜中的反常霍尔效应（AHE）对微观结构和磁性均匀性高度敏感。然而，人们对渗流阈值附近的微观结构和形态的演化，以及它与低维磁性异质结构中产生的磁性和磁输运行为的联系仍然知之甚少。在这项研究中，我们通过改变 Fe 层厚度，对 Si/Fe 双层的结构、微观结构和磁输运特性的演变进行了全面分析。 X 射线衍射 (XRD)、高分辨率透射电子显微镜 (HRTEM) 和磁化数据揭示了当 tFe 降至 30 埃以下时，渗流驱动的从连续金属膜到晶粒渗流网络结构的转变。涉及纵向电阻率 (rho) 和反常霍尔电阻率 (rho_A,h,s) 的传输测量在渗滤阈值附近显示出明显的发散。与电子和磁性组合的 rho_A,h,s 相比，纯电子传导通道 (rho) 的演化更加缓慢。对结构、磁性和磁输运数据的渗透分析产生了 0.78 至 1.16 范围内的临界指数，与二维无序系统的临界指数一致。 rho_A,h,s 和 rho 之间的 AHE 比例关系揭示了 AHE 机制的交叉，从厚低电阻样品 (tFe > 30 埃) 中具有较小偏斜散射分量 (n ~ 1.42) 的混合本征/侧跳贡献到高阻薄膜 (tFe <= 30 ) 中的偏斜散射主导机制 (n = 0.62)安斯特罗姆）。这种交叉与晶粒之间结构和磁性连接的开始同时发生。此外，这些发现强调了渗流框架下微观结构、形态、磁性和霍尔传输之间的相互联系。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.07115v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The anomalous Hall effect (AHE) in magnetic nanofilms is highly sensitive to the microstructural and magnetic homogeneity. However, the evolution of the microstructure and morphology near the percolation threshold, and its connection to the resulting magnetic and magnetotransport behavior in low-dimensional magnetic heterostructures, remain poorly understood. In this study, we present a comprehensive analysis of the evolution of the structural, microstructural, and magnetotransport properties of Si/Fe bilayers by varying the Fe layer thickness. X-ray diffraction (XRD), high-resolution transmission electron microscopy (HRTEM) and magnetisation data reveal a percolation-driven transition from a continuous metallic film to percolative network structure of grains when tFe decreases below 30 Angstrom. Transport measurements involving longitudinal resistivity (rho), and the anomalous Hall resistivity (rho_A,h,s) show clear divergence near the percolation threshold. The purely electronic conduction channels (rho) evolve more gradually as compared to the combined electronic and magnetic ones rho_A,h,s. The percolative analysis of the structural, magnetic, and magnetotransport data yields a critical exponent in the range of 0.78 to 1.16, consistent with that of 2D-disordered systems. The AHE scaling relation between the rho_A,h,s and rho reveals a crossover of the AHE mechanism from a mixed intrinsic/side-jump contribution with a minor skew scattering component (n ~ 1.42) in the thick, low-resistive samples (tFe > 30 Angstrom) to a skew-scattering-dominant mechanism (n = 0.62) in the high-resistive films (tFe <= 30 Angstrom). This crossover coincides with the onset of structural and magnetic connectivity between the grains. Furthermore, these findings underscore the interlink between microstructure, morphology, magnetism, and Hall transport under a percolation framework.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.07128v1 发布类型：新 摘要：半金属具有理想的 100% 自旋极化，被广泛认为是自旋电子和量子技术的关键材料；然而，半金属态本质上是脆弱的，因为它依赖于交换分裂和能带填充的微妙平衡，因此非常容易受到无序、外部扰动和热效应的影响。在这里，我们引入了隐藏半金属性的概念，即对称强制净零磁化磁体的整体电子结构是非半金属的，而其两个对称相关扇区中的每一个都是单独的半金属性，从而通过层自由度实现稳健的 100% 自旋极化。至关重要的是，整个系统消失的净磁化抑制了杂散场和磁不稳定性，使半金属功能本质上比传统的铁磁半金属更强大。使用第一性原理计算，我们在 PT 对称双层 CrS₂ 中演示了这种机制，并进一步表明外部电场驱动系统进入看似禁止的完全补偿亚铁磁金属，其中隐藏的半金属性仍然存在。最后，我们简要确认了交替磁体中隐藏半金属性的实现，通过将其嵌入对称保护的隐藏扇区中来建立稳定半金属行为的通用范式，并为设计和发现前所未有的半金属相开辟了新途径。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.07128v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Half-metals, featuring ideal 100% spin polarization, are widely regarded as key materials for spintronic and quantum technologies; however, the half-metallic state is intrinsically fragile, as it relies on a delicate balance of exchange splitting and band filling and is therefore highly susceptible to disorder, external perturbations, and thermal effects. Here we introduce the concept of hidden half-metallicity, whereby the global electronic structure of a symmetry-enforced net-zero-magnetization magnet is non-half-metallic, while each of its two symmetry-related sectors is individually half-metallic, enabling robust 100% spin polarization through a layer degree of freedom. Crucially, the vanishing net magnetization of the entire system suppresses stray fields and magnetic instabilities, rendering the half-metallic functionality inherently more robust than in conventional ferromagnetic half-metals. Using first-principles calculations, we demonstrate this mechanism in a PT-symmetric bilayer CrS₂, and further show that an external electric field drives the system into a seemingly forbidden fully compensated ferrimagnetic metal in which hidden half-metallicity persists. Finally, we briefly confirm the realization of hidden half-metallicity in altermagnets, establishing a general paradigm for stabilizing half-metallic behavior by embedding it in symmetry-protected hidden sectors and opening a new route toward the design and discovery of unprecedented half-metallic phases.

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.07138v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Motivated by recent advances in the study of altermagnetism, or unconventional magnetism, and in the realization and manipulation of two-impurity Kondo physics in real materials, we propose a phase-sensitive method to explore unconventional magnetic symmetries. Our method can be implemented with spin-resolved scanning tunneling microscopy to study two-impurity Kondo phenomena on altermagnetic metals by varying the distance and orientation between magnetic impurities. Using quantum Monte Carlo simulations, we analyze the spin splitting of the Kondo resonance, whose spatial distribution sensitively captures the symmetry of the underlying altermagnetic order. Furthermore, the impurity spin correlations reflects the anisotropy of the RKKY interaction due to the altermagnetic Fermi surface splitting. This work provides a framework for studying the competition between the Kondo effect, the RKKY interaction and altermagnetism, in the simplest possible system.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.07255v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们利用漫射和非弹性 X 射线散射以及拉曼光谱研究了 SmNiC₂ 中电荷密度波 (CDW) 不稳定性和铁磁性之间的相互作用。我们识别出驱动不相称 CDW (I-CDW) 的软声学声子，并发现其他 RNiC₂ 成员（R= 稀土）中稳定的相称 CDW (C-CDW) 波矢处的第二个科恩异常。两种声子的显着软化及其随温度的对比演化揭示了两种有序趋势之间的竞争。除了区域中心和软声子的温度依赖性的明显异常之外，我们还观察到 CDW 的集体振幅模式，随着铁磁性的出现，它突然崩溃。令人惊讶的是，尽管费米表面嵌套条件恶化，科恩异常仍然保持在铁磁性状态。我们的实验结果得到了从头计算的支持，强调了电子-声子相互作用在驱动 CDW 形成和调整竞争电荷与磁序之间的平衡方面的核心作用。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.07255v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We investigate the interplay between charge density wave (CDW) instabilities and ferromagnetism in SmNiC₂ using diffuse and inelastic x-ray scattering together with Raman spectroscopy. We identify a soft acoustic phonon driving the incommensurate CDW (I-CDW) and uncover a second Kohn anomaly at the wave vector of the commensurate CDW (C-CDW) stabilized in other RNiC₂ members (R= rare earth). The marked softening of both phonons and their contrasting evolution with temperature reveal a competition between the two ordering tendencies. Alongside pronounced anomalies in the temperature dependence of the zone center and soft phonons, we observe the collective amplitude mode of the CDW, which collapses abruptly as ferromagnetism sets in. Surprisingly, the Kohn anomalies persist in the ferromagnetic state despite the degradation of Fermi-surface nesting conditions. Our experimental findings, supported by ab initio calculations, highlight the central role of the electron-phonon interaction in driving the CDW formation and tuning the balance between competing charge and magnetic orders.

中文摘要

arXiv:2601.07275v1 公告类型：新 摘要：具有非零贝里曲率的磁性拓扑材料因其特殊的磁电耦合现象和在下一代自旋电子器件中的潜在应用而成为深入研究的焦点。在这项工作中，我们成功合成了高质量的 GdAlSi 单晶，它是 RAlX（R = 稀土元素；X = Si/Ge）家族的典型成员，理论上预测其能够维持非平凡的 Weyl 半金属态。通过对磁性和输运特性的系统研究，我们确定了临界温度 TN1 31.9 K 和 TN2 31.1 K 下的两个连续反铁磁转变，如温度相关电阻率、磁化率和比热测量所证明的那样。值得注意的是，超过 8 T 的外加磁场会引发第三次磁转变 (TN3)，产生一系列变磁转变，共同形成树枝状相图。这种复杂的磁性行为归因于局域 Gd-4f 矩和巡回传导电子之间的相互作用，可能是由 Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya 相互作用介导的。输运测量揭示了跨越相边界时磁阻的显着逐步异常，并伴随着磁矩翻转过程产生的明显磁滞回线。我们的结果不仅将 GdAlSi 确立为研究相关拓扑态的丰富平台，而且还证明了其通过外尔半金属磁对称操纵来工程拓扑相变的潜力。

English Abstract

arXiv:2601.07275v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Magnetic topological materials hosting non-zero Berry curvature have emerged as a focus of intensive research due to their exceptional magnetoelectric coupling phenomena and potential applications in next-generation spintronic devices. In this work, we successfully synthesized high-quality GdAlSi single crystals, a prototypical member of RAlX (R = rare earth elements; X = Si/Ge) family that has been theoretically predicted to sustain a non-trivial Weyl semimetal state. Through systematic investigations of magnetic and transport properties, we identified two successive antiferromagnetic transitions at critical temperatures TN1 31.9 K and TN2 31.1 K, as evidenced by temperature-dependent resistivity, magnetic susceptibility, and specific heat measurements. Notably, applied magnetic fields exceeding 8 T induce a third magnetic transition (TN3), generating a cascade of metamagnetic transitions that collectively form a dendritic phase diagram. This complex magnetic behavior is attributed to the interplay between localized Gd-4f moments and itinerant conduction electrons, possibly mediated by Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions. Transport measurements revealed striking stepwise anomalies in magnetoresistance when crossing phase boundaries, accompanied by pronounced hysteresis loops arising from magnetic moment flopping processes. Our results not only establish GdAlSi as a rich platform for investigating correlated topological states, but also demonstrate its potential for engineering topological phase transitions through magnetic symmetry manipulation in Weyl semimetals.
